|14163|dividehex|Bug 1491948: adds single-request-reopen resolv.conf          On centos 6 hosts, this ensures the 'single-request-reopen'         option is included in resolv.conf which alleviates the issue of         dns queries being lost when two requests are sent back to back         from the same socket.  The symptom being a ~5 sec dns reply         delay.          For more information, see:         http://man7.org/linux/man-pages/man5/resolv.conf.5.html         https://unix.stackexchange.com/questions/290987/resolving-hostname-takes-5-seconds|[URL](https://github.com/mozilla-releng/build-puppet/commit/3f806432282e71525be7e02fe6a21cb90a5ff992)|2018-09-18 16:39:04

|13808|escapewindow|use fqdn for ssl cert definition  The self-signed ssl certs are fqdn-specific, so it doesn't make a lot of sense to allow for them to cross domains based on shared hostname.  Also, `hiera_hash` appears to reference the global hiera secrets and doesn't respect environments. Switching to `secret` instead appears to work and also respect the environment.  This change assumes we're going to switch over the secrets at the same time we land this patch set. If we want a more gradual change over, we may want to introduce a new set of secrets (e.g., `signing_server_ssl_cert_new` ?) that can coexist with the old secrets.|[URL](https://github.com/mozilla-releng/build-puppet/commit/e8fd287691cd7582caf510fbb5cdead1f6f804c7)|2018-07-21 00:56:45

|12966|escapewindow|bug 1421124 - create a new python27 module. r=callek  We're creating a new module here so we don't upgrade the world. Instead, each module can point at the python27 module when they're ready.  This patch is intended to upgrade virtualenv and pip from our ancient pip 1.5.5 to virtualenv 15.0.2 + pip 8.1.2. I chose this version because virtualenv 15.1.0 includes pip 9.0.1; pip 9.x requires SSL; and our puppet servers don't have valid SSL certs. pip 8.1.2 allows for --trusted-host which allows us to fix the puppet bustage in this bug, but avoids requiring new SSL certs on the puppet servers.
